***tongs.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tongs.html>tongs</a> (112163)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:tong.html>tong</a> ("<a href = vnd.unilang:tool.html>tool</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:for.html>for</a> manipulating <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fire.html>fire</a>") + -s
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***tosti.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tosti.html>tosti</a> (32233)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosti.html>tosti</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:toast.html>toast</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toast.html>toast</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:first.html>First</a> attested <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:late.html>late</a> 1950s.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosti.html>tosti</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosti.html>tosti</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:s.html>s</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:chiefly.html>chiefly</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> toasted <a href = vnd.unilang:sandwich.html>sandwich</a> containing <a href = vnd.unilang:cheese.html>cheese</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:usually.html>usually</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ham.html>ham</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> optionally <a href = vnd.unilang:other.html>other</a> ingredients <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> condiments; <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> toastie.

***totdat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:totdat.html>totdat</a> (966)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a></i>.
